country_event = { # Strike
	id = ukrpol.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.6" }
	title = ukrpol.6.t
	desc = ukrpol.6.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_strike

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_path
			}
		}
		UKR_decrease_direktoria = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_minor_concessions
			days = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_king_path }
			UKR_increase_king_strength = yes
			UKR_increase_workers_opinion_king = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_king = yes
		}
		else = {
			UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_increase_workers_opinion_hetman = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_hetman = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.6.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
		227 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 1
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.07
		UKR_decrease_direktoria = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_general_strike
			days = 14
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_king_path }
			clear_variable = UKR_workers_alignment
			UKR_increase_king_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_king = yes
			UKR_increase_Protofis_opinion_king = yes
		}
		else = {
			clear_variable = UKR_workers_alignment
			UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
			UKR_increase_Protofis_opinion_hetman = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.6.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
		}
		227 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 1
			}
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 1
			}
		}
		UKR_increase_direktoria = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_general_strike_big
			days = 30
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_king_path }
			clear_variable = UKR_workers_alignment
			UKR_decrease_king_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_king = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_king = yes
		}
		else = {
			clear_variable = UKR_workers_alignment
			UKR_decrease_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_hetman = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Dualism
	id = ukrpol.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.10" }
	title = ukrpol.10.t
	desc = ukrpol.10.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 10000
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UMP
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_USKHD
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_UVO_KON
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_UVO_MELNYK
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_UVO_DONTSOV
					}
				}
			}
		}			
		set_country_flag = UKR_king_path
		complete_national_focus = UKR_King_Path
		add_ideas = UKR_dualism
		set_variable = { political_power_ideology = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		map_party_popularity_PP_gain_to_ideology = yes
		set_power_balance = {
			id = UKR_dualism
			left_side = UKR_king_side 
			right_side = UKR_hetman_side
			set_value = 0.05
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ukrpol.12
			days = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 10000
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_HETMAN_DEM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_HETMAN_AUT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_LEO_STEFAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_DANYLO
					}
				}
			}
		}			
		set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_path
		complete_national_focus = UKR_Hetman_Path
		add_ideas = UKR_dualism
		set_power_balance = {
			id = UKR_dualism
			left_side = UKR_king_side 
			right_side = UKR_hetman_side
			set_value = 0.05
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ukrpol.26
			days = 5
		}		
	}

country_event = { # Melnyk Returns
	id = ukrpol.13
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.13" }
	title = ukrpol.13.t
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.13.d.king
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = UKR_King_Path }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.13.d.hetman
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = UKR_King_Path }
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_melnyk
	
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.13.a
		set_global_flag = WSU_totalist_uvo
		UPR = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 17905 }
				set_nationality = ROOT
				clr_unit_leader_flag = UVO_Galicia_leader
			}
		}
		UPR = {
			clr_country_flag = UPR_melnyk_on_our_side
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = -0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = 0.03
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 17917 }
					promote_leader = yes
					custom_effect_tooltip = will_become_uvo_leader_galicia
					set_unit_leader_flag = UVO_Galicia_leader
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = leftist_uvo_becomes_dominant_galicia
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mykola Stsiborskyi"
				desc = "POLITICS_MYKOLA_STSIBORSKYI_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Mykola_Stsiborskyi.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"

				}
				set_party_name = {

					name = UKR_totalist_party3
					long_name = UKR_totalist_party3_long
				}
				set_party_name = {

country_event = { # End of the Hetmanate
	id = ukrpol.25
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.25" }
	title = ukrpol.25.t
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.25.d.uvo
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_With_UVO }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.25.d
		trigger = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_With_UVO } }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_lypky
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = UKR
		has_government = paternal_autocrat
		OR = {
			power_balance_value = {
				id = UKR_dualism
				value < 0
			}
			check_variable = { UKR_society_support > 0 }
		}
		NOT = { 
			power_balance_value = {
				id = UKR_dualism
				value > 0
			} 
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.25.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_path }
			clr_country_flag = UKR_hetman_path
			set_country_flag = UKR_king_path
		}
		default_party_popularity_PP_gain = yes
		set_global_flag = UKR_hetmanate_is_over
		UKR_decrease_hetman_strength = yes
		UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
		remove_power_balance = { id = UKR_dualism }
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 17909 }
			retire = yes
		}
		#event_target:UKR_Pavlo_Skoropadskyi = { retire = yes }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.15
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
		remove_ideas = UKR_derzhavna_varta
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_With_UVO
					has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_Wih_UDP
				}
			}
			add_ideas = {
				UKR_Vasyl_Vyshyvanyi_hog_ade
				UKR_Kazymyr_Huzhkovskyi_for_ade
				UKR_Omelian_Senyk_eco_npo
				UKR_Dmitri_Dontsov_sec_npo
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ukrpol.34
				days = 3
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				end_coalition = yes
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = {
				UKR_Vasyl_Vyshyvanyi_hog_ade
				UKR_Serhiy_Shemet_for_ade
				UKR_Mykhailo_Savur_Tsypriianovych_eco_ade
				UKR_Yulian_Romanchuk_sec_ade
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ukrpol.152
				days = 3
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = UPR_dyrektoria_become_exiled_in_WSU
					NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_dyrektoria_uprising_active }
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = UKR_dualism
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = UKR_dualism
				add_idea = UKR_political_instability
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = UKR_UMP_USKhD_Coalition
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = ukrpol.76
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}						
}

				}

					is_owned_by = GAL

					}
				}
			}

			ROOT = { add_state_claim = PREV }
		}

				limit = {

						OR = {
							is_owned_by = FROM
							is_owned_by = GAL

								is_owned_by = POL
								POL = { is_ally_with = FROM }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				BUK = {
					transfer_state = 713

				}
				FROM = {
					puppet = BUK
				}
				BUK = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
			}
		}
		add_ideas = UKR_austrian_trade
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_returned_land
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM

		}

	}

country_event = { # Regency Council
	id = ukrpol.121
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.121" }
	title = ukrpol.121.t
	desc = ukrpol.121.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.121.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { UKR_regency_leo_stefan > UKR_regency_danilo }
					check_variable = { UKR_regency_leo_stefan > UKR_regency_pavlo }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { UKR_regency_pavlo > UKR_regency_danilo }
					check_variable = { UKR_regency_pavlo > UKR_regency_leo_stefan }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_will_become_hetmanate }
				}
			}
		}
		UKR_create_leo_stefan = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_will_become_hetmanate }
			set_cosmetic_tag = UKR_hetmanate
			add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
			hidden_effect = {
				get_current_government_type = yes
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberal }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = market_liberal }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_trait = UKR_king_title
			hidden_effect = {
				get_current_government_type = yes
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberal }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_king_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = market_liberal }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_king_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_king_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_king_title
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = UKR_regency_council
		set_country_flag = UKR_regency_council_over
		country_event = {
			id = ukrpol.122
			days = 2
		}
	}

		trigger = {

				transfer_state = PREV

					target = AUS

				}
			}
		}
		UKR = { leave_faction = yes }

			limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			add_to_faction = UKR
		}
		else = {
			create_faction = dniep_danubian_alliance
			add_to_faction = UKR
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = POL
					tag = GAL
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = AUS
				modifier = KR_outraged
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = UKR
				modifier = KR_outraged
			}
		}

		}

			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.12
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.08
			}
		}	
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Ivan Poltavets-Ostrianytsia"
			desc = "POLITICS_IVAN_POLTAVETS_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Ivan_Poltavets_Ostrianytsia.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = pataut_cossack_subtype
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_template = "Kozatska Dyviziia" }
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Kozatska Dyviziia"
				division_names_group = UKR_CAV_02
				regiments = {
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				}
				support = {
					recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Kozatska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
				owner = ROOT
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Kozatska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
				owner = ROOT
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Kozatska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
				owner = ROOT
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Kozatska Dyviziia\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
				owner = ROOT
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			name = UKR_paternal_autocrat_party4
			long_name = UKR_paternal_autocrat_party4_long
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = UKR_cossack_state
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = UKR_khmel_host } }
			add_ideas = UKR_khmel_host			
			UKR_improve_ukrainisation = yes
		}		
	}

	id = ukrsoc.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.1" }
	immediate = { set_country_flag = UKR_can_secure_power }
	title = ukrsoc.1.t
	desc = ukrsoc.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_dyrektoria
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.1.a
		set_country_flag = UKR_natpops_in_opposition
		set_variable = { UVO_dont_like_it = 1 }
		add_ideas = UKR_political_instability_dyrektoria
		country_event = {
			id = ukrsoc.2
			days = 5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrmisc.42
				days = 10
				random_days = 30
			}
		}
	}	
}

					}

					}

					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_PEOPLES_REPUBLIC option = UKR_FUTURE_SHUMSKYI_DICTATOR }

					}

					}

					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_PEOPLES_REPUBLIC

					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_PEOPLES_REPUBLIC

			}

		}

		text = ukrsoc.72.t.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.72.d.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.72.d.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.72.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
		add_political_power = 25
		set_global_flag = KCN_research_yes			
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = kyiv_conf_research
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote }
			}
			country_event = ukrsoc.73
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
					is_in_tech_research_group = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 2 }
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.KCN_voters
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.73 days = KCN_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
					is_in_tech_research_group = no
				}
				set_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 2 }
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.KCN_voters
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.74 days = KCN_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
			}
		}			
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.72.b
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
	}	
}

country_event = { #Membership - voting
	id = ukrsoc.77
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.77 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ukrsoc.77.t
	desc = ukrsoc.77.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yes
		name = KCN_vote_yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_continent_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { any_owned_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_owned_state = { 
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
						is_core_of = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#No
		name = KCN_vote_no
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { any_owned_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				any_owned_state = { 
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
						is_core_of = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = no }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_no_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#Abstain
		name = KCN_vote_abstain
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_continent_as_ROOT = no }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_abstain_votes = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { # UKP 
	id = ukrsoc.113
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.113" }
	title = ukrsoc.113.t
	desc = ukrsoc.113.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.113.a
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_in_faction_with = INT }
			}
			INT = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		}
		else = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			give_guarantee = FROM
			FROM = { give_guarantee = ROOT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { has_government = totalist }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				name = UKR_radical_socialist_party
				long_name = UKR_radical_socialist_party_long
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mykola Skrypnyk"
				desc = "POLITICS_MYKOLA_SKRYPNYK_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Mykola_Skrypnyk.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = national_communism_subtype
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsoc.117
				days = 180
				random_days = 300
			}
		}
	}		
}

country_event = { # USDRP
	id = ukrsoc.152
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.152" }
	title = ukrsoc.152.t
	desc = ukrsoc.152.d
	trigger = {
		UKR_usdrp_in_power = yes	
	}
		
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_no_more_loans }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget > 0 }
				check_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget < 11 }
			}
			check_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget < 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.152.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_pop_change = -10 }
		UKR_increase_red_kyiv_popularity = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full
				days = 180
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate
				days = 180
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Navodnytskyi_Mist }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Navodnytskyi_Mist
				days = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Renovate_Velykyi_Mykola }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Renovate_Velykyi_Mykola
				days = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Karl_Marx_Monument }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Karl_Marx_Monument
				days = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Metro_Construction }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Metro_Construction
				days = 150
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Open_Shevchenko_State_Art_School }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Open_Shevchenko_State_Art_School
				days = 15
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line
				days = 30
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsoc.152
				days = 90
				random_days = 220
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_Borrow_money_tt
		add_to_variable = { var = UKR_kyiv_budget_debt value = 40 }
		multiply_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget_debt = 1.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Repay_money }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = UKR_Repay_money
				days = 180
			}
		}
		else = { activate_mission = UKR_Repay_money }
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.152.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}		
		set_country_flag = UKR_no_more_loans
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 25
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_pop_change = 5 }
		UKR_increase_red_kyiv_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_budget_monthly_change = -5 }
		UKR_increase_kyiv_budget_monthly_by_sum = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full }
			remove_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate }
			remove_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Metro_Construction }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Metro_Construction
				days = 150
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line }
			remove_decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line
		}		
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_budget_change = 40 }
		UKR_increase_kyiv_budget_by_sum = yes
	}		
}

country_event = { # UPSR
	id = ukrsoc.179
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.179" }
	title = ukrsoc.179.t
	desc = ukrsoc.179.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.179.a
		set_country_flag = UKR_upsr_is_radsoc
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		UKR_move_upsr_leader_to_radsoc = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_socdem_half_pop = party_popularity@social_democrat }
		multiply_temp_variable = { UKR_socdem_half_pop = 50 }
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_socdem_to_radsoc_value = party_popularity@social_democrat }
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_socdem_to_radsoc_value_reverse = 0 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { var = UKR_socdem_to_radsoc_value_reverse value = party_popularity@social_democrat }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = UKR_socdem_to_radsoc_value_reverse }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = UKR_socdem_to_radsoc_value }
		set_political_party = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = UKR_socdem_half_pop
		}
		
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:syndicalist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Levko Kovaliv"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_ideas = {
				UKR_Dmytro_Isaievych_for_sde
				UKR_Panas_P_Lyubchenko_eco_rso
				UKR_Hryhorii_Hrynko_sec_rso
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = {
				UKR_Levko_Kovaliv_for_rso
				UKR_Panas_P_Lyubchenko_eco_rso
				UKR_Hryhorii_Hrynko_sec_rso
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			name = UKR_syndicalist_party3
			long_name = UKR_syndicalist_party3_long
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			name = UKR_syndicalist_party3
			long_name = UKR_syndicalist_party3_long
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Volodymyr Vynnychenko"
				desc = "POLITICS_VOLODYMYR_VYNNYCHENKO_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Volodymyr_Vynnychenko.png" 
				expire = "1965.1.1"

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.372" }
	title = ukrsoc.372.t
	desc = ukrsoc.372.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_khruschev3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.372.a
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = UKR_nuclear_threats
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = ukrsoc.373
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_actual_major = yes
					has_socialist_government = no
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = FROM
					modifier = UKR_nuclear_threats
				}				
			}
		}
	}
}

		set_country_flag = UKR_BLMON

			}

			}

		}
	}

country_event = { # Agricultural crisis!
	id = ukreco.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukreco.2" }
	title = ukreco.2.t
	desc = ukreco.2.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukreco.2.a
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = UKR_GER_no_help_agr_crisis
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.25
		set_country_flag = UKR_agriculture_crisis
		UKR_fire_agricultural_crisis = yes
		add_ideas = UKR_village_outflow
		UKR_increase_direktoria = yes
		country_event = {
			id = ukreco.5
			days = 3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = crm.3
				days = 5
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ukrmisc.25
				days = 32
			}	
			UPR = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = GER
					modifier = UKR_GER_no_help_agr_crisis
				} # -10
			}		
		}
		
	}
}

country_event = { # Leave Mitteleuropa?
	id = ukreco.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukreco.5" }

	desc = ukreco.5.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukreco.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {

						rule = UKR_FUTURE

					}

						rule = UKR_FUTURE

					}

						rule = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING
						option = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING_DYREKTORIA_PEACE_GA
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING
						option = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING_DYREKTORIA_GUARANTEED
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING
						option = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING_DYREKTORIA_PEACE_GI
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING
						option = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING_DYREKTORIA_WAR_GA
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING
						option = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING_DYREKTORIA_WAR_GI
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_has_left_mitteleuropa
		add_stability = 0.05
		UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
		UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
		UKR_increase_direktoria = yes
		GER_leave_mitteleuropa = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = ukreco.5.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_UMP
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_FUTURE
						option = UKR_FUTURE_KING_USKHD
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		UKR_decrease_hetman_strength = yes
		UKR_increase_king_strength = yes
		UKR_increase_king = yes
		UKR_decrease_direktoria = yes
	}
}

### Land Reform ###
country_event = { # End of Reform?
	id = ukreco.25
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukreco.25" }
	title = ukreco.25.t
	desc = ukreco.25.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukreco.25.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Borotbysts < 30 }
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Popularity > 75 }
				check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Success > 75 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Socialization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_socialization_of_land
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Municipalization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_municipalization_of_land
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Nationalization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_nationalisation_of_land
			}
			else = { add_ideas = UKR_successful_land_reform_plan_excellent }
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
			UKR_breadbasket_remove_consumer_goods = yes
			UKR_breadbasket_add_monthly_population = yes
			UKR_breadbasket_remove_supply_consumption = yes
			UKR_breadbasket_remove_resource_penalty = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Popularity > 50 }
				check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Success > 50 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Socialization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_socialization_of_land
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Municipalization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_municipalization_of_land
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_Nationalization_Land }
				add_ideas = UKR_nationalisation_of_land
			}
			else = { add_ideas = UKR_successful_land_reform_plan_good }
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_breadbasket_of_europe_will_change
			UKR_breadbasket_remove_consumer_goods = yes
			UKR_breadbasket_add_monthly_population = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = UKR_successful_land_reform_plan_decent
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_LandReform_Success
		set_country_flag = UKR_disable_borotbist_uprisings
		clr_country_flag = LandReformBegunUKR
		remove_ideas = UKR_land_reform
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_land_reform_modifier }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = UKR_borotbyst_uprising_state
				}
			}
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
			remove_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = UKR_borotbyst_uprising_state
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukreco.25.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { UKR_Land_Reform_Borotbysts > 29 }
		}
		add_stability = -0.15
		clr_country_flag = LandReformBegunUKR
		remove_ideas = UKR_land_reform
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_land_reform_modifier }
		country_event = {
			id = ukrsoc.200
			days = 5
		}
	}
}

		}

				id = ukrfor.101
				days = 4
			}
		}

					}

			NOT = {
				any_allied_country = {
					has_capitulated = yes
					capital_scope = {
						controller = { is_ally_with = FROM }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrfor.114.d.losing_ground
		trigger = {
			any_allied_country = {
				has_capitulated = yes
				capital_scope = {
					controller = { is_ally_with = FROM }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_war_with = FROM
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
					has_capitulated = yes
					capital_scope = {
						controller = { is_ally_with = FROM }
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = capitulated_ally
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.114.a #We have no choice...
		FROM = { country_event = ukrfor.115 }
	}

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.114.b #We will not negotiate with syndicalists!
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = -0.1
		FROM = { country_event = ukrfor.116 }
	}
}

			95 = {
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_full_control_of_state = 1088 }

				transfer_state_to = ROOT
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_full_control_of_state = 1220 }
			1220 = {
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_full_control_of_state = 1221 }
			1221 = {
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_full_control_of_state = 137 }
			137 = {
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}		
		FROM = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_dyrektoria_tree_unlocked
				NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_congress_begins }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsoc.1
				days = 5
			}
		}
		
	}

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.115.b #No peace with the imperialists!
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = -0.1
		FROM = { country_event = ukrfor.116 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Ultimatum for Cholm
	id = ukrfor.200
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.200" }
	title = ukrfor.200.t
	desc = ukrfor.200.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.200.a #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				1088 = {
					owner = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
			}
			1088 = {
				owner = {
					country_event = {
						id = ukrfor.203
						days = 1
						random = 24
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = UKR
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = FROM
						is_claimed_by = FROM
					}
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrfor.201
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.200.b #refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrfor.202
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #owner accepts
	id = ukrfor.201
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.201" }
	title = ukrfor.201.t
	desc = ukrfor.201.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrfor.201.a #great
		FROM = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						AND = {
							is_claimed_by = ROM
							ROOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROM }
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
}

		text = ukrfor.253.d.RUS
		trigger = { FROM = { tag = RUS } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrfor.253.d.POL
		trigger = { FROM = { tag = POL } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrfor.253.d.WHR
		trigger = { FROM = { tag = WHR } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrfor.253.d.ROM
		trigger = { FROM = { tag = ROM } }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.253.a
		trigger = { 
			FROM = { 
				OR = {
					tag = GER 
					tag = RUS
				}
			}
			UKR_petliura_in_power = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_petliura_shumskyi }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_petliura_shumskyi_united_front }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_duumvirate_colapsed }			
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = UKR_foreign_intervention } }
			add_ideas = UKR_foreign_intervention
		}
		USR = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrfor.260
				days = 2
			}
		}			
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.253.e
		trigger = { 
			FROM = { tag = GER }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 65
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = UKR_foreign_intervention } }
			add_ideas = UKR_foreign_intervention
		}
		add_war_support = 0.02				
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.253.c	
		trigger = { 
			FROM = { NOT = { tag = GER } }
			NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					ROOT_is_threatened_cautious = yes
					FROM = { dont_start_major_faction_wars = yes }
					FROM = { default_attack_AI_trigger_FROM = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = UKR_foreign_intervention } }
			add_ideas = UKR_foreign_intervention
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.253.b		
		trigger = { 
			FROM = { NOT = { tag = GER } }
			NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		if = {

			add_ideas = UKR_foreign_intervention
		}
		add_war_support = 0.02
		add_stability = -0.03
	}

			has_war_with = FROM
		}

country_event = { #PS - Czechoslovakia Result
	id = ukrfor.27
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.27" }
	title = ukrfor.27.t
	desc = ukrfor.27.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Approved!
		name = ukrfor.27.a
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent
			set_country_flag = czechoslovakia_independent_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_separate_independent
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_separate_independent
			set_country_flag = czechoslovakia_separate_approved
		}
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = ukrfor.27.b
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent
		clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_separate_independent
		set_country_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_denied
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Panslavic Congress - Galicia
	id = ukrfor.22
	title = ukrfor.22.t
	desc = ukrfor.22.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			RUS = {
				has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
			}
			OR = {
				UKR = {
					has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
				}
				GAL = {
					has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
				}
				POL = {
					has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
				}
				AUS = {
					has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.22.a
		trigger = {
			country_exists = POL
			country_exists = UKR
			UKR = {
				has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
			}
			POL = {
				has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}		
		activate_mission = PSC_vote_timer
		set_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
		set_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = ukrfor.26
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ukrfor.31
			days = 15
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.22.b
		trigger = {
			country_exists = POL
			NOT = { country_exists = UKR }
			POL = {
				has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}		
		activate_mission = PSC_vote_timer
		set_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
		set_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = ukrfor.26
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ukrfor.31
			days = 15
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.22.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {country_exists = POL }
			10 = {
				owner = {
					tag = RUS
				}
			}
			NOT = { country_exists = UKR }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		activate_mission = PSC_vote_timer
		set_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
		set_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = ukrfor.26
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ukrfor.31
			days = 15
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.22.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = UKR }
			
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}
		activate_mission = PSC_vote_timer
		set_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_split
		set_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = ukrfor.26
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ukrfor.31
			days = 15
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.22.f
		trigger = {
			country_exists = POL
			POL = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = psc_council_vote }
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
			country_exists = UKR
			UKR = {

			factor = 25

country_event = { #PS - Galicia Result
	id = ukrfor.31
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.31" }
	title = ukrfor.31.t
	desc = ukrfor.31.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Approved!
		name = ukrfor.27.a
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
			set_country_flag = galicia_split_ukraine_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
			set_country_flag = galicia_split_russia_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
			set_country_flag = galicia_annex_russia_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_split
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_split
			set_country_flag = eastgalicia_split_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_ukraine
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_ukraine
			set_country_flag = eastgalicia_ukraine_approved
		}
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = ukrfor.27.b
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_ukraine
		clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
		clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
		clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
		clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_split
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Free Czechoslovakia
	id = ukrfor.1305
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.1305" }
	title = ukrfor.1305.t
	desc = ukrfor.1305.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.1305.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = czechoslovakia_independent_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CZE
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			CZE = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Johann II zu Schwarzenberg"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						has_country_flag = CZE_SVK_was_puppeted
						}
					}
					effect_tooltip = { kill_country_leader = yes }
				}
			set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_czechoslavakia
			
			leave_faction = yes
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = czechoslovakia_separate_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CZE
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CZE
				}
					CZE = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			CZE = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Johann II zu Schwarzenberg"
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							has_country_flag = CZE_SVK_was_puppeted
							}
						}
						effect_tooltip = { kill_country_leader = yes }
					}
				
				leave_faction = yes
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SVK = { is_subject_of = AUS }
				}
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = SVK
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
				SVK = { 
					leave_faction = yes
					separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						SVK = { NOT = { owns_state = 664 } }
					}
					SVK = {
						transfer_state = 664
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				AUS = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = SVK
						}
					}
					SVK = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = SVK
						}
					}
					SVK = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = zakarpatie_cze_approved }
			}
			CZE = {
				transfer_state = 73
				transfer_state = 1119
				add_state_core = 73
				add_state_core = 1119
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = zakarpatie_slo_approved }
			}
			SVK = {
				transfer_state = 73
				transfer_state = 1119
				add_state_core = 73
				add_state_core = 1119
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

			factor = 45
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50

				id = ukrfor.1315
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Free Illyria
	id = ukrfor.1315
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.1315" }
	title = ukrfor.1305.t
	desc = ukrfor.1305.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.1305.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = illyria_independent_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CRO = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CRO
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = CRO
							is_core_of = SLO
							is_core_of = BOS
							is_core_of = MNT
						}
					}
					CRO = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = AUS
				}
			}
			CRO = { 
				leave_faction = yes
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = illyria_slovenia_croatia_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CRO = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CRO
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = CRO
							is_core_of = BOS
						}
					}
					CRO = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = AUS
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 102
							state = 1101
							state = 1103
							state = 1104
							state = 736
							state = 1100
							state = 1144
						}
					}
					SLO = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = AUS
				}
			}
			CRO = { 
				leave_faction = yes
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = illyria_separate_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CRO = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CRO
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = CRO
					}
					CRO = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = AUS
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 102
							state = 1101
							state = 1103
							state = 1104
							state = 736
							state = 1100
							state = 1144
						}
					}
					SLO = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = AUS
				}
			}
			CRO = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						state = 104
					}
					BOS = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = CRO
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						state = 105
					}
					MNT = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = CRO
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = vojvodina_croatia_approved }
			}
			CRO = {
				transfer_state = 45
				add_state_core = 73
				transfer_state = 45
				add_state_core = 875
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrfor.1318.d.croatia
		trigger = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vojvodina_croatia_approved }
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {

						id = ukrfor.1319
						days = 5
					}
				}

				}

		}

						OR = {
							is_core_of = CRO
						}
					}
					SER = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = AUS
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						state = 102
					}
					SER = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = AUS
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # Ukraine Wants to Join the International
	id = ukraine.37
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukraine.37" }
	title = ukraine.37.t
	desc = ukraine.37.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukraine.37.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_to_faction = UKR
		hidden_effect = {
			UKR = {
				country_event = {
					days = 1
					id = ukraine.38
				}
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = UKR
			modifier = UKR_FRA_accepted_us
		} # 100
	}

	option = {
		name = ukraine.37.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		add_stability = -0.02
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = UKR
			modifier = UKR_FRA_refused_us
		} # -100
	}
}

country_event = { # Ukraine Join the International
	id = ukraine.38
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukraine.38" }
	title = ukraine.38.t
	desc = ukraine.38.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukraine.38.a
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = UKR_GER_CAN_joined_inter
		} # -150
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CAN
			modifier = UKR_GER_CAN_joined_inter
		} # -150
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = ENT
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = ENT
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KR_outraged
			}
			embargo_ROOT = yes
		}
	}
}

	id = ukraine.71
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukraine.71" }
	title = ukraine.71.t
	desc = ukraine.71.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukraine.71.a
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = AUS } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 85 }
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = no }
			create_faction = "Russian Alliance"
		}
		GER = { remove_from_faction = UKR }
		add_to_faction = UKR
		hidden_effect = {
			UKR = {
				country_event = {
					days = 2
					id = ukraine.72
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ukraine.71.a
		trigger = { tag = AUS }
		ai_chance = { factor = 85 }

		add_to_faction = UKR
		hidden_effect = {
			UKR = {

					days = 2
					id = ukraine.75

			}
		}

country_event = { # Ukraine in Russian alliance
	id = ukraine.72
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukraine.72" }
	title = ukraine.72.t
	desc = ukraine.72.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukraine.72.a
		set_country_flag = UKR_NORTHERN_WIND
		add_ideas = UKR_Ties_Russia
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CRM
				CRM = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
						is_subject_of = RUS
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = CRM
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					days = 4
					id = ukraine.73
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
